  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function () {
        $("#btnSerach").click(searchKey);
        //回车快捷查询 
        $("#wd").keypress(function (e) {
            var keyCode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which ? e.which : e.charCode;
            if (keyCode == 13) {
                searchKey();
            }
        });
    });

    function searchKey() {
        if ($.trim($("#wd").val()) != "请输入搜索关键字" && $.trim($("#wd").val()) != "") {
            var typeName = $(".header_search_t_l").find("span").text();
            if (typeName == "产品") {
                window.open("http://s.51sole.com/s.aspx?q=" + $.trim(encodeURIComponent($("#wd").val())));
            } else { window.open("http://pindaoye.51sole.com/search.aspx?wd=" + encodeURI($.trim($("#wd").val()))); }
        }
    }
  </script>

 <script type="text/javascript">
  $(function () {
        GetInquiryList();

        $(".nav_hy_b").addClass("show");

        var swiper = new Swiper(".i_banner", {
            simulateTouch: false,//禁止PC端拖动
            speed: 500,
            autoplay: 6000,
            mode: "horizontal",
            loop: true,
            autoplayDisableOnInteraction: false,
            onSlideChangeStart: function (swiper) {
                var i = parseInt(swiper.activeLoopIndex);
                $(".i_banner_nav a").removeClass("on");
                $(".i_banner_nav").find("a").eq(i).addClass("on");
            },
        })

        $(".i_banner_nav a").hover(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $(".i_banner_nav a").removeClass('on');
            $(this).addClass('on');
            swiper.swipeTo($(this).index());
        })

        $(".banner_l").hover(function () {
            swiper.stopAutoplay();
        }, function () {
            swiper.startAutoplay();
        });

        $(".i_lc_c_chart").each(function () {
            var id = $(this).attr("id");
            echartFun(id);
        });

        var xjdtGd = setInterval('infoAuto(".i_xjdt_r_b")', 5000);
        $(".i_xjdt_r_b").hover(function () {
            clearInterval(xjdtGd);
        }, function () {
            xjdtGd = setInterval('infoAuto(".i_xjdt_r_b")', 5000);
        });

        $(".i_cphyTab").hover(function () {
            $(".i_cphyTab").removeClass("i_cphyTab_on");
            $(this).addClass("i_cphyTab_on");
            var i = parseInt($(this).index()) - 1;
            $(".i_cphy_box").find(".i_cphy").removeClass("show");
            $(".i_cphy_box").find(".i_cphy").eq(i).addClass("show");
        });

        $(".i_yqljTab").hover(function () {
            $(".i_yqljTab").removeClass("i_yqljTab_on");
            $(this).addClass("i_yqljTab_on");
            var i = parseInt($(this).index()) - 1;
            $(".i_yqlj_box").find(".i_yqlj").removeClass("show");
            $(".i_yqlj_box").find(".i_yqlj").eq(i).addClass("show");
        });

        $('.i_navTab').find('a').click(function () {
            $("html,body").stop(true);
            var to = parseInt($('.i_navTab_info').eq($(this).index()).offset().top) - 10;
            $('html,body').animate({ 'scrollTop': to }, 500)
        });
        
        iNavTab();
    });

    $(window).scroll(function () {
        iNavTab();
    });

    function iNavTab() {
        var scroH = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (scroH > 520) {
            $(".i_navTab").show();
        } else {
            $(".i_navTab").hide();
        }
    }

    //信息滚动
    function infoAuto(obj) {
        var a = parseInt($(obj).find("li:first").css('height'));
        $(obj).find("ul:first").animate({
            marginTop: "-" + a + ""
        }, 500, function () {
            $(this).css({ marginTop: "0px" }).find("li:first").appendTo(this);
        });
    }

    function echartFun(id) {
        var dom1 = document.getElementById(id);
        var myChart1 = echarts.init(dom1);
        myChart1.setOption(option = {
            title: {
                text: '',
                show: false
            },
            tooltip: {
                trigger: 'axis'
            },
            legend: {
                right: 0,
            },
            grid: {
                top: '30px',
                left: '10px',
                right: '1px',
                bottom: '0',
                containLabel: true
            },
            xAxis: {
                name: '日期',
                nameLocation: "start",
                nameGap: "5",
                nameTextStyle: { padding: [27, 0, 0, 0] },
                type: 'category',
                axisLine: { lineStyle: { color: "#999" } },
                axisTick: { alignWithLabel: true },
                data: ['02-01', '02-02', '02-03', '02-04', '02-05', '02-06', '02-07', '02-08', '02-09', '02-10', '02-11', '02-12', '02-13', '02-14', '02-15']
            },
            yAxis: {
                type: 'value',
                name: '订单数',
                splitNumber: '3',
                axisLine: { lineStyle: { color: "#999" } },
                splitLine: { show: false }
            },
            series: [
                {
                    name: '收到订单',
                    type: 'line',
                    data: [587, 351, 401, 525, 387, 704, 532, 397, 499, 451, 666, 502, 498, 365, 537],
                    itemStyle: { color: "#037BCE" },
                }, {
                    name: '成交订单',
                    type: 'line',
                    data: [360, 128, 291, 234, 190, 380, 310, 128, 291, 234, 402, 343, 256, 171, 290],
                    itemStyle: { color: "#ED59A4" },
                }
            ]
        });
    }

  <span class="qwtg_close">

 <script type="text/javascript">
  $('.qwtg_close').click(function () {
        $(".qwtg_right").remove();
        return false;
    });

 <!-- 底部推广广告small -->
 <script type="text/javascript">
  var qwtg = 0;
    $(function () {
        $('.qwtg_close').click(function () {
            $(".qwtg_right").remove();
            return false;
        });

        $('.qwtg_left').click(function () {
            qwtg = 1;
            showqwtg();
        });
        $('.qwtg_xx').click(function () {
            qwtg = 1;
            hideqwtg();
        });

        scrollshowqwtg();
    });
    $(window).scroll(function () {
        scrollshowqwtg();
    });

    $(".i_lc_c_chart").each(function () {
        var id = $(this).attr("id");
        var _fid = $(this).attr("data-floorid");

        $.ajax({
            url: "/GPYG/GPYG_Handler.ashx?method=GetIndexFloorData",
            type: "POST",
            data: { fid: _fid },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data) {
                if (data.state == "true") {
                    var re = data.msg;
                    var arr = re.split('∑');
                    dateArr = arr[0].split(',');
                    rArr = arr[1].split(',');
                    tArr = arr[2].split(',');
                    echartFun(id, dateArr, rArr, tArr);
                }
            }
        });
    });

    function echartFun(id, dateArr, rArr, tArr) {
        var dom1 = document.getElementById(id);
        var myChart1 = echarts.init(dom1);
        myChart1.setOption(option = {
            title: {
                text: '',
                show: false
            },
            tooltip: {
                trigger: 'axis'
            },
            legend: {
                right: 0,
            },
            grid: {
                top: '30px',
                left: '10px',
                right: '1px',
                bottom: '0',
                containLabel: true
            },
            xAxis: {
                name: '日期',
                nameLocation: "start",
                nameGap: "5",
                nameTextStyle: { padding: [27, 0, 0, 0] },
                type: 'category',
                axisLine: { lineStyle: { color: "#999" } },
                axisTick: { alignWithLabel: true },
                data: dateArr
            },
            yAxis: {
                type: 'value',
                name: '订单数',
                splitNumber: '3',
                axisLine: { lineStyle: { color: "#999" } },
                splitLine: { show: false }
            },
            series: [
                {
                    name: '收到订单',
                    type: 'line',
                    data: rArr,
                    itemStyle: { color: "#037BCE" },
                }, {
                    name: '成交订单',
                    type: 'line',
                    data: tArr,
                    itemStyle: { color: "#ED59A4" },
                }
            ]
        });
    }

    function showqwtg() {
        $('.qwtg_left').stop().animate({ left: "-200px" }, 600);
        $('.qwtg').stop().animate({ bottom: "0" }, 600);
    }
    function hideqwtg() {
        $('.qwtg_left').stop().animate({ left: "0" }, 600);
        $('.qwtg').stop().animate({ bottom: "-300px" }, 600);
    }
    function scrollshowqwtg() {
        if (qwtg == 0) {
            var scroH = $(window).scrollTop();
            if (scroH > 700) {
                showqwtg();
            } else {
                hideqwtg();
            }
        }
    }

    function check() {
        var qwtg = $(".qwtg_select").val();
        if (qwtg == "请选择您的服务项目") {
            alert("请选择您的服务项目");
            return false;
        }
        var Mobiphone = $("#txtmobile");
        var regMobiphone = /[0-9]{9,12}/;
        if (Mobiphone.val() == "") {
            alert("请输入手机号码！");
            Mobiphone.focus();
            return false;
        }
        if (!regMobiphone.test(Mobiphone.val())) {
            alert("请输入正确的手机号码！");
            Mobiphone.focus();
            return false;
        }
        PostData(qwtg, Mobiphone.val());
    }

    function PostData(qwtg, Mobiphone) {
        var chkData = $.ajax({
            url: "/activity/douyin/postDataHandle.ashx?opt=saveinfo",
            async: false, error: function () { },
            data: { txtcontent: qwtg, txtmobile: Mobiphone, FromID: 70 }
        });
        var dataValue = chkData.responseText;
        if (dataValue == "1") {
            alert("您的申请已成功发送！");
            $("#txtmobile").val("");
        } else {
            alert("对不起！您的申请发送失败！");
        }
    }

    function GetInquiryList() {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/GPYG/GPYG_Handler.ashx?method=GetInquiryList",
            type: "POST",
            data: {},
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (re) {
                if (re.state == "true") {
                    var _html = "";
                    var list = re.data.list;
                    for (var i = 0; i < list.length; i++) {
                        var info = list[i];
                        _html += "<li class='clearfix'>" +
                            "<div class='i_x_i i_x_n1'>" + info.IsUrgentStr + info.PulishDate + "</div>" +
                            "<div class='i_x_i i_x_n2'><span class='hswz'>" + info.PurchaseTitle + "</span></div>" +
                            //"<div class='i_x_i i_x_n3'>" + info.CompanyName + "</div>" +
                            //"<div class='i_x_i i_x_n4'>" + info.OfferCount + "条</div>" +
                            "<div class='i_x_i i_x_n5'>" + info.ProductKinds + "种</div>" +
                            "<div class='i_x_i i_x_n6'>" + info.RemainingTime + "</div>" +
                            "<div class='i_x_i i_x_n7'>" + info.PurchaseStatusName + "</div>" + "</li>";
                    }

                    $("#InquiryList").html(_html);
                }
            }
        });
    }
 </script>
</html>
